<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user initiated a session with a primary goal of implementing a robust, end-to-end tracking layer for their Landing Pages (LPs). This involved creating a script to handle session initialization, visitor tracking (), comprehensive UTM parameter capture, and reliable CTA click tracking using . The user emphasized the need for this system to be 100% reliable, deterministic, and free of legacy code.

Following the successful implementation and multiple rounds of auditing of the tracking layer (v2.1), the user requested further critical enhancements:
1.  **Mandatory LP-Form Linking**: Enforce a strict business rule where a Landing Page must always be linked to a Form, and a Form cannot be created without being linked to an LP. This was to ensure data integrity and prevent orphan leads.
2.  **UI Simplification**: A radical simplification of the UI for creating LPs. The user wanted a 10-15 second creation flow, requiring only three user inputs (Name, URL, Product Type), with all other configuration (form creation, linking, script injection) happening automatically in the background.
3.  **Permanent Standards**: The user requested that key principles (UI simplicity, zero-legacy versioning, mandatory E2E testing) be formally documented and adopted as permanent standards for all future development.
4.  **Full Business Validation**: A final end-to-end test of the entire lead funnel (LP -> CTA -> Form -> Submit -> CRM Delivery) to ensure not just technical correctness but also business logic integrity, including delivery to external CRMs (ZR7 and MDL).

**User's preferred language**: French

**what currently exists?**
The application now features a fully implemented and heavily audited **RDZ Tracking Layer v2.1**. This system is embedded into the  service and handles the entire visitor lifecycle on LPs, from session creation to CTA clicks, using  for reliability. The backend endpoints in  have been updated to be tolerant of 's content types. All legacy logic and unused code ( guards, old Pydantic models) have been removed.

A strict business rule now enforces that LPs and Forms must be linked. The backend (, ) rejects any attempt to create a standalone form or unlink an existing pair. The frontend UI () has been updated to reflect this, guiding users to create new pairs from the Landing Pages screen.

The LP creation process () has been radically simplified. A new modal allows users to create a complete, ready-to-use LP and its associated Form by filling out just three fields, with all technical configuration and linking handled automatically.

Permanent development standards have been documented in .

This test simulated the entire lead funnel from LP creation to lead submission, with the goal of verifying that the lead was correctly created in the internal CRM and that routing logic for external CRMs (ZR7, MDL) was triggered. The test confirmed the lead was created correctly internally, but could not confirm successful delivery to external CRMs due to a lack of configured API keys in the environment.

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

  async def test_1_lp_visits(session):
      """Test 1: 10 LP visits avec 10 sessions diffrentes  10 events reus"""
      print("\n" + "="*60)
      print("TEST 1: 10 LP Visits  10 Events Backend")
      print("="*60)

      for i in range(10):
          # Crer une session unique
          session_data = {
              "lp_code": f"LP-TEST-{i+1:03d}",
              "form_code": "PV-TEST-001",
              "utm_campaign": f"test_visit_{i+1}"
          }

          async with session.post(f"{BASE_URL}/track/session", json=session_data) as resp:
              data = await resp.json()
              session_id = data.get("session_id")

              if session_id:
                  results["test_1_lp_visits"]["sent"] += 1

                  # Envoyer lp-visit
                  visit_data = {
                      "session_id": session_id,
                      "lp_code": f"LP-TEST-{i+1:03d}",
                      "utm_campaign": f"test_visit_{i+1}"
                  }

                  # Simuler sendBeacon (text/plain)
                  async with session.post(
                      f"{BASE_URL}/track/lp-visit",
                      data=json.dumps(visit_data),
                      headers={"Content-Type": "text/plain;charset=UTF-8"}
                  ) as visit_resp:
                      visit_result = await visit_resp.json()

                      if visit_result.get("success"):
                          if visit_result.get("duplicate"):
                              results["test_1_lp_visits"]["duplicates"] += 1
                          else:
                              results["test_1_lp_visits"]["received"] += 1
                          print(f"   Visit {i+1}: session={session_id[:8]}... event={visit_result.get('event_id', 'N/A')[:8]}...")

      sent = results["test_1_lp_visits"]["sent"]
      received = results["test_1_lp_visits"]["received"]
      print(f"\n  Rsultat: {received}/{sent} events reus")
      return received == sent

  async def test_2_multi_tab(session):
      """Test 2: Simulation multi-tab avec mme visitor_id  session unique rutilise"""
      print("\n" + "="*60)
      print("TEST 2: Multi-Tab  Session Unique")
      print("="*60)

      # Simuler un visitor_id fixe (comme un cookie)
      visitor_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
      lp_code = "LP-MULTITAB-TEST"

      # Simuler 5 "onglets" ouvrant la mme LP rapidement
      for tab in range(5):
          session_data = {
              "lp_code": lp_code,
              "form_code": "PV-MULTITAB",
              "utm_campaign": "multitab_test"
          }

          # Le backend vrifie visitor_id via cookie, simulons avec header custom pour test
          async with session.post(
              f"{BASE_URL}/track/session",
              json=session_data,
              cookies={"_rdz_vid": visitor_id}
          ) as resp:
              data = await resp.json()
              session_id = data.get("session_id")
              reused = data.get("reused", False)

              results["test_2_multi_tab"]["sessions_created"] += 1
              results["test_2_multi_tab"]["unique_sessions"].add(session_id)

              status = "REUSED" if reused else "NEW"
              print(f"  Tab {tab+1}: session={session_id[:8]}... ({status})")

      unique = len(results["test_2_multi_tab"]["unique_sessions"])
      total = results["test_2_multi_tab"]["sessions_created"]
      print(f"\n  Rsultat: {unique} session(s) unique(s) pour {total} requtes")

      # Le backend devrait rutiliser la session dans les 30 minutes
      return unique == 1

  async def test_3_cta_spam(session):
      """Test 3: Spam clicks CTA  1 seul vnement enregistr"""
      print("\n" + "="*60)
      print("TEST 3: CTA Spam Clicks  Single Event")
      print("="*60)

      # Crer une session
      session_data = {
          "lp_code": "LP-SPAM-TEST",
          "form_code": "PV-SPAM-TEST"
      }

      async with session.post(f"{BASE_URL}/track/session", json=session_data) as resp:
          data = await resp.json()
          session_id = data.get("session_id")

      print(f"  Session cre: {session_id[:8]}...")

      # Simuler 20 clicks rapides (spam)
      for click in range(20):
          event_data = {
              "session_id": session_id,
              "event_type": "cta_click",
              "lp_code": "LP-SPAM-TEST"
          }

          async with session.post(
              f"{BASE_URL}/track/event",
              data=json.dumps(event_data),
              headers={"Content-Type": "text/plain"}
          ) as resp:
              result = await resp.json()
              results["test_3_cta_spam"]["clicks_sent"] += 1

              if result.get("success"):
                  if result.get("duplicate"):
                      results["test_3_cta_spam"]["duplicates"] += 1
                  else:
                      results["test_3_cta_spam"]["events_recorded"] += 1

      sent = results["test_3_cta_spam"]["clicks_sent"]
      recorded = results["test_3_cta_spam"]["events_recorded"]
      duplicates = results["test_3_cta_spam"]["duplicates"]

      print(f"  Clicks envoys: {sent}")
      print(f"  Events enregistrs: {recorded}")
      print(f"  Duplicates rejets: {duplicates}")
      print(f"\n  Rsultat: {recorded} event(s) pour {sent} clicks")

      return recorded == 1 and duplicates == sent - 1

_____________________ ERROR at setup of test_4_full_funnel _____________________
file /app/backend/tests/test_tracking_reliability.py, line 176
  async def test_4_full_funnel(session, iterations=100):
      """Test 4: Full funnel LP  CTA  Form  Submit  100"""
      print("\n" + "="*60)
      print(f"TEST 4: Full Funnel  {iterations} Iterations")
      print("="*60)

      for i in range(iterations):
          results["test_4_funnel"]["started"] += 1

          try:
              # 1. Crer session (LP)
              session_data = {
                  "lp_code": f"LP-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}",
                  "form_code": f"PV-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}",
                  "liaison_code": f"LP-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}_PV-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}",
                  "utm_campaign": f"funnel_test_{i+1}",
                  "utm_source": "test",
                  "utm_medium": "reliability"
              }

              async with session.post(f"{BASE_URL}/track/session", json=session_data) as resp:
                  data = await resp.json()
                  session_id = data.get("session_id")
                  if not session_id:
                      results["test_4_funnel"]["errors"].append(f"Iteration {i+1}: No session_id")
                      continue

              # 2. LP Visit
              visit_data = {
                  "session_id": session_id,
                  "lp_code": f"LP-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}",
                  "utm_campaign": f"funnel_test_{i+1}"
              }
              async with session.post(
                  f"{BASE_URL}/track/lp-visit",
                  data=json.dumps(visit_data),
                  headers={"Content-Type": "text/plain"}
              ) as resp:
                  lp_result = await resp.json()
                  if not lp_result.get("success"):
                      results["test_4_funnel"]["errors"].append(f"Iteration {i+1}: LP visit failed")
                      continue

              # 3. CTA Click
              cta_data = {
                  "session_id": session_id,
                  "event_type": "cta_click",
                  "lp_code": f"LP-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}"
              }
              async with session.post(
                  f"{BASE_URL}/track/event",
                  data=json.dumps(cta_data),
                  headers={"Content-Type": "text/plain"}
              ) as resp:
                  cta_result = await resp.json()
                  if not cta_result.get("success"):
                      results["test_4_funnel"]["errors"].append(f"Iteration {i+1}: CTA click failed")
                      continue

              # 4. Form Start
              form_start_data = {
                  "session_id": session_id,
                  "event_type": "form_start",
                  "form_code": f"PV-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}"
              }
              async with session.post(
                  f"{BASE_URL}/track/event",
                  data=json.dumps(form_start_data),
                  headers={"Content-Type": "text/plain"}
              ) as resp:
                  form_result = await resp.json()
                  if not form_result.get("success"):
                      results["test_4_funnel"]["errors"].append(f"Iteration {i+1}: Form start failed")
                      continue

              # 5. Submit Lead
              lead_data = {
                  "session_id": session_id,
                  "form_code": f"PV-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}",
                  "lp_code": f"LP-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}",
                  "liaison_code": f"LP-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}_PV-FUNNEL-{i+1:03d}",
                  "utm_campaign": f"funnel_test_{i+1}",
                  "phone": f"06{i:08d}",  # Numros uniques
                  "nom": f"TestFunnel{i+1}",
                  "prenom": "Reliability",
                  "departement": "75",
                  "email": f"test{i+1}@reliability.test"
              }

              async with session.post(f"{BASE_URL}/leads", json=lead_data) as resp:
                  lead_result = await resp.json()
                  if lead_result.get("success"):
                      results["test_4_funnel"]["leads_created"] += 1
                      results["test_4_funnel"]["completed"] += 1
                  else:
                      results["test_4_funnel"]["errors"].append(f"Iteration {i+1}: Lead failed - {lead_result}")

          except Exception as e:
              results["test_4_funnel"]["errors"].append(f"Iteration {i+1}: Exception - {str(e)}")

          # Progress
          if (i + 1) % 10 == 0:
              print(f"  Progress: {i+1}/{iterations} ({results['test_4_funnel']['completed']} completed)")

      started = results["test_4_funnel"]["started"]
      completed = results["test_4_funnel"]["completed"]
      leads = results["test_4_funnel"]["leads_created"]
      errors = len(results["test_4_funnel"]["errors"])

      print(f"\n  Started: {started}")
      print(f"  Completed: {completed}")
      print(f"  Leads created: {leads}")
      print(f"  Errors: {errors}")

      if errors > 0:
          print(f"\n  First 5 errors:")
          for err in results["test_4_funnel"]["errors"][:5]:
              print(f"    - {err}")

      success_rate = (completed / started) * 100 if started > 0 else 0
      print(f"\n  Success Rate: {success_rate:.1f}%")

      return completed == started

          ("text/plain;charset=UTF-8", "sendBeacon default"),
          ("text/plain", "sendBeacon variant"),
          ("application/json", "fetch standard"),
      ]

                  text = await resp.text()

                      status = ""

                  print(f"  {description} ({ct}): {status}")

              results["test_5_fallback"]["fetch_fallback"] += 1

      success = results["test_5_fallback"]["success"]
      total = results["test_5_fallback"]["fetch_fallback"]

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?
